(\n\t\"context\"\n\t\"net/http\"\n\t\"net/http/httptest\"\n\t\"testing\"\n\n\t\"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert\"\n\t\"github.com/stretchr/testify/require\"\n\t\"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/server/authn/method\"\n\t\"google.golang.org/grpc/metadata\"\n)\n\n// TestRegression_CookieTokenNotExtracted demonstrates that the ForwardCookies function\n// has a bug where it doesn't properly forward the flipt_client_token cookie to gRPC metadata.\n// This prevents browser-based sessions from working since HTTP cookies are not extracted\n// and forwarded correctly.\nfunc TestRegression_CookieTokenNotExtracted(t *testing.T) {\n\tconst (\n\t\tclientToken = \"test_token_12345\"\n\t\tstateCookie = \"state_cookie_value\"\n\t)\n\n\t// Create a test HTTP request with both state and client token cookies\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: clientToken,\n\t})\n\n\t// Call ForwardCookies to convert HTTP cookies to gRPC metadata\n\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t// BUG: The current implementation doesn't properly forward cookies to the expected metadata key\n\t// The gRPC middleware expects cookies to be forwarded as individual cookie values, but\n\t// ForwardCookies has it's not\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// This is what actually happens - cookies are not forwarded to the right metadata key\n\t\tt.Logf(\"No cookies found in grpcgateway-cookie metadata\")\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: Cookies are not being forwarded to gRPC metadata as expected\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Also verify that the metadata was populated at all\n\t// The bug in line 49 of http.go always uses stateCookieKey instead of the current key\n\tif len(md) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: ForwardCookies returned empty metadata - cookies not forwarded at all\")\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestRegression_ForwardCookiesBugDetails demonstrates the exact bug in the ForwardCookies function.\n// The function iterates over cookie keys (stateCookieKey and tokenCookieKey) but always\n// sets the metadata using stateCookieKey, overwriting entries instead of properly forwarding them.\nfunc TestRegression_ForwardCookiesBugDetails(t *testing.T) {\n\tconst (\n\t\tstateCookieValue = \"state123\"\n\t\ttokenCookieValue = \"token456\"\n\t)\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://localhost/test\", nil)\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_state\",\n\t\tValue: stateCookieValue,\n\t})\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: tokenCookieValue,\n\t})\n\n\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t// When ForwardCookies processes cookies, it:\n\t// 1. Iterates through [stateCookieKey, tokenCookieKey]\n\t// 2. Extracts each cookie value\n\t// 3. BUT: Always sets md[stateCookieKey] regardless of which key is being processed\n\n\t// This means:\n\t// - When processing stateCookieKey, it sets md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = stateCookieValue\n\t// - When processing tokenCookieKey, it sets md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = tokenCookieValue (WRONG!)\n\t// The tokenCookieKey value overwrites the stateCookieKey entry due to the bug\n\n\t// Due to the bug, we expect that md will have wrong keys/values:\n\tstateValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_state\")\n\n\tif len(stateValues) > 0 {\n\t\t// This might contain the token value instead of the state value due to the bug\n\t\t// The last value would be from processing tokenCookieKey\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Value at flipt_client_state key: %v\", stateValues[0])\n\t\tif stateValues[0] == tokenCookieValue {\n\t\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: Token cookie overwrote state cookie in metadata due to bug in ForwardCookies\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Try to access the metadata using the correct key for token\n\ttokenValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_token\")\n\tif len(tokenValues) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: No flipt_client_token key in metadata - ForwardCookies bug prevents proper forwarding\")\n\t}\n\n\t// The expected behavior would be:\n\t// - md[\"grpcgateway-cookie\"] = [\"flipt_client_state=state123; flipt_client_token=token456\"]\n\t// OR individual entries:\n\t// - md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = [\"state123\"]\n\t// - md[\"flipt_client_token\"] = [\"token456\"]\n\t// But the current implementation doesn't properly forward to the gRPC middleware's expected format\n}\n\n// TestRegression_ServerAuthenticationSkipNotConfigured demonstrates that while servers\n// can implement the SkipsAuthenticationServer interface, there's no mechanism to register\n// them with the authentication middleware to actually skip authentication.\n// This means even \"public\" servers that should not require authentication still have\n// authentication enforced on them.\nfunc TestRegression_ServerAuthenticationSkipNotConfigured(t *testing.T) {\n\t// The SkipsAuthenticationServer interface exists and is implemented by public.Server\n\t// but in internal/cmd/authn.go, when authenticationGRPC() is called, the\n\t// WithServerSkipsAuthentication option is never used to register servers.\n\n\t// This means:\n\t// 1. Public authentication methods (like ListAuthenticationMethods) should not require auth\n\t// 2. But there's no mechanism to bypass the AuthenticationRequiredInterceptor\n\t// 3. The skipped() function in middleware.go checks if a server implements\n\t//    SkipsAuthenticationServer, but servers are never registered with this option\n\n\t// Verify that WithServerSkipsAuthentication option exists\n\tvar opts []interface{}\n\t// This function exists but is never called in the registration code\n\t// opts = append(opts, grpc_middleware.WithServerSkipsAuthentication(publicServer))\n\n\t// Without calling WithServerSkipsAuthentication during setup, the middleware has no way\n\t// to know which servers should skip authentication, and the skipped() function will\n\t// always return false for the skipped servers slice check.\n\n\t// The expected behavior would be:\n\t// 1. Public servers implement SkipsAuthenticationServer\n\t// 2. They should be registered with WithServerSkipsAuthentication during middleware setup\n\t// 3. The middleware's skipped() function should check the interface AND the registered list\n\n\t// But currently step 2 is missing, so all servers require authentication\n\n\tt.Log(\"REGRESSION: Server-level authentication skip mechanism exists but is not configured\")\n\tt.Log(\"Public servers implement SkipsAuthenticationServer interface\")\n\tt.Log(\"But WithServerSkipsAuthentication is never called during middleware setup\")\n\tt.Log(\"This means public servers are incorrectly forced to require authentication\")\n}\n\n// TestRegression_CookieForwardingToGRPCMetadata tests the integration between\n// HTTP cookies and gRPC metadata forwarding for the gRPC-gateway.\nfunc TestRegression_CookieForwardingToGRPCMetadata(t *testing.T) {\n\t// The gRPC middleware expects cookies to be available as gRPC metadata\n\t// with the key \"grpcgateway-cookie\" to parse them properly\n\n\tconst clientToken = \"valid_token_xyz789\"\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://localhost/api/v1/flags\", nil)\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: clientToken,\n\t})\n\n\t// Convert HTTP cookies to gRPC metadata\n\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t// Check the actual structure of the returned metadata\n\tt.Logf(\"Forwarded metadata keys: %v\", md)\n\tt.Logf(\"Metadata content: %#v\", map[string][]string(md))\n\n\t// The gRPC middleware's cookieFromMetadata function expects:\n\t// md.Get(\"grpcgateway-cookie\") to return cookie header values\n\t// which it then parses with http.Cookie\n\n\tcookieHeaders := md.Get(\"grpcgateway-cookie\")\n\n\t// The issue: ForwardCookies should create a proper \"Cookie\" header string\n\t// that can be parsed by the gRPC middleware, but it doesn't do this correctly\n\n\tif len(cookieHeaders) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: No grpcgateway-cookie metadata entry - cookies not forwarded\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// The cookie header should contain \"flipt_client_token=value\"\n\t\t// But due to the bug, this is not properly constructed\n\t\tfound := false\n\t\tfor _, header := range cookieHeaders {\n\t\t\tif header == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tt.Logf(\"Cookie header: %s\", header)\n\t\t\t// The middleware's cookieFromMetadata then parses this with:\n\t\t\t// (&http.Request{Header: http.Header{\"Cookie\": values}}).Cookie(key)\n\t\t\t// This should work if the Cookie header is properly formatted\n\t\t\tif _, err := http.ParseCookie(header); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tt.Logf(\"Cookie header is not properly formatted: %v\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfound = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif !found {\n\t\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: Cookie headers are empty or malformed\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// TestRegression_HTTPCookieAuthenticationNotWorking tests that HTTP requests\n// with authentication tokens in cookies are rejected because the cookies\n// are not properly extracted and forwarded to the gRPC authentication middleware.\nfunc TestRegression_HTTPCookieAuthenticationNotWorking(t *testing.T) {\n\t// This is the high-level integration test showing the overall issue:\n\t// 1. Browser makes HTTP request with flipt_client_token cookie\n\t// 2. gRPC-gateway converts this to gRPC call\n\t// 3. ForwardCookies should forward the cookie to gRPC metadata\n\t// 4. gRPC middleware should extract and validate the token\n\t// 5. Request should succeed with authentication\n\n\t// But step 3 fails, so step 4 never gets the token, and step 5 fails\n\n\tconst clientToken = \"browser_session_token\"\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://localhost/api/v1/flags\", nil)\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: clientToken,\n\t})\n\n\t// Step 3: Forward cookies to gRPC metadata\n\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t// After forwarding, the gRPC middleware should be able to extract the token\n\t// by calling clientTokenFromMetadata(md), which expects:\n\t// - Either Authorization header with \"Bearer token\"\n\t// - Or grpcgateway-cookie with \"flipt_client_token=token\"\n\n\tif len(md) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: Forwarded metadata is empty - HTTP cookie authentication cannot work\")\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if the cookie is in the expected format for gRPC middleware\n\tcookieVals := md.Get(\"grpcgateway-cookie\")\n\tif len(cookieVals) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: Cookie not forwarded as grpcgateway-cookie metadata\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// The gRPC middleware expects to parse this as HTTP cookie header(s)\n\t\t// It should contain the flipt_client_token cookie\n\t\thasTokenCookie := false\n\t\tfor _, cookieStr := range cookieVals {\n\t\t\tif cookieStr == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Try to parse as HTTP Cookie header\n\t\t\t// Should be able to extract flipt_client_token=value\n\t\t\tif _, err := http.ParseCookie(cookieStr); demonstrates the exact bug in the ForwardCookies function.\n// The function iterates over cookie keys (stateCookieKey and tokenCookieKey) but always\n// sets the metadata using stateCookieKey, overwriting entries instead of properly forwarding them.\nfunc TestRegression_ForwardCookiesBugDetails(t *testing.T) {\n\tconst (\n\t\tstateCookieValue = \"state123\"\n\t\ttokenCookieValue = \"token456\"\n\t)\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://localhost/test\", nil)\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_state\",\n\t\tValue: stateCookieValue,\n\t})\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: tokenCookieValue,\n\t})\n\n\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t// When ForwardCookies processes cookies, it:\n\t// 1. Iterates through [stateCookieKey, tokenCookieKey]\n\t// 2. Extracts each cookie value\n\t// 3. BUT: Always sets md[stateCookieKey] regardless of which key is being processed\n\n\t// This means:\n\t// - When processing stateCookieKey, it sets md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = stateCookieValue\n\t// - When processing tokenCookieKey, it sets md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = tokenCookieValue (WRONG!)\n\t// The tokenCookieKey value overwrites the stateCookieKey entry due to the bug\n\n\t// Due to the bug, we expect that md will have wrong keys/values:\n\tstateValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_state\")\n\n\tif len(stateValues) > 0 {\n\t\t// This might contain the token value instead of the state value due to the bug\n\t\t// The last value would be from processing tokenCookieKey\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Value at flipt_client_state key: %v\", stateValues[0])\n\t\tif stateValues[0] == tokenCookieValue {\n\t\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: Token cookie overwrote state cookie in metadata due to bug in ForwardCookies\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Try to access the metadata using the correct key for token\n\ttokenValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_token\")\n\tif len(tokenValues) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: No flipt_client_token key in metadata - ForwardCookies bug prevents proper forwarding\")\n\t}\n\n\t// The expected behavior would be:\n\t// - md[\"grpcgateway-cookie\"] = [\"flipt_client_state=state123; flipt_client_token=token456\"]\n\t// OR individual entries:\n\t// - md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = [\"state123\"]\n\t// - md[\"flipt_client_token\"] = [\"token456\"]\n\t// But the current implementation doesn't properly forward to the gRPC middleware's expected format\n}\n\n// TestRegression_ServerAuthenticationSkipNotConfigured demonstrates that while servers\n// can implement the SkipsAuthenticationServer interface, there's no mechanism to register\n// them with the authentication middleware to actually skip authentication.\n// This means even \"public\" servers that should not require authentication still have\n// authentication enforced on them.\nfunc TestRegression_ServerAuthenticationSkipNotConfigured(t *testing.T) {\n\t// The SkipsAuthenticationServer interface exists and is implemented by public.Server\n\t// but in internal/cmd/authn.go, when authenticationGRPC() is called, the\n\t// WithServerSkipsAuthentication option is never used to register servers.\n\n\t// This means:\n\t// 1. nil)\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_state\",\n\t\tValue: stateCookie,\n\t})\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: {\n\t\t\tt.Log(\"State value is correct, but token value is missing\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(tokenValues) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: flipt_client_token key not found in metadata - tokens function iterates over cookie keys (stateCookieKey and tokenCookieKey) but always\n// sets the metadata using stateCookieKey, overwriting entries instead of properly forwarding them.\nfunc TestRegression_ForwardCookiesBugDetails(t *testing.T) {\n\tconst (\n\t\tstateCookieValue = \"state123\"\n\t\ttokenCookieValue = \"token456\"\n\t)\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://localhost/test\", nil)\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_state\",\n\t\tValue: stateCookieValue,\n\t})\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: tokenCookieValue,\n\t})\n\n\tmd := ForwardCookies_Buggy(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t// When ForwardCookies processes cookies, it:\n\t// 1. Iterates through [stateCookieKey, tokenCookieKey]\n\t// 2. Extracts each cookie value\n\t// 3. BUT: Always sets md[stateCookieKey] regardless of which key is being processed\n\n\t// This means:\n\t// - When processing stateCookieKey, it sets md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = stateCookieValue\n\t// - When processing tokenCookieKey, it sets md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = tokenCookieValue (WRONG!)\n\t// The tokenCookieKey value overwrites the stateCookieKey entry due to the bug\n\n\t// Due to the bug, we expect that md will have wrong keys/values:\n\tstateValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_state\")\n\n\tif len(stateValues) > 0 {\n\t\t// This might contain the token value instead of the state value due to the bug\n\t\t// The last value would be from processing tokenCookieKey\n\t\tt.Logf(\"Value at flipt_client_state key: %v\", stateValues[0])\n\t\tif stateValues[0] == tokenCookieValue {\n\t\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: Token cookie overwrote state cookie in metadata due to bug in ForwardCookies\")\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Try to access the metadata using the correct key for token\n\ttokenValues := md.Get(\"flipt_client_token\")\n\tif len(tokenValues) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: No flipt_client_token key in metadata - ForwardCookies bug prevents proper forwarding\")\n\t}\n\n\t// The expected behavior would be:\n\t// - md[\"grpcgateway-cookie\"] = [\"flipt_client_state=state123; flipt_client_token=token456\"]\n\t// OR individual entries:\n\t// - md[\"flipt_client_state\"] = [\"state123\"]\n\t// - md[\"flipt_client_token\"] = [\"token456\"]\n\t// But the current implementation doesn't properly forward to the gRPC middleware's expected format\n}\n\n// TestRegression_ServerAuthenticationSkipNotConfigured demonstrates that while servers\n// can implement the SkipsAuthenticationServer interface, there's no mechanism to register\n// them with the authentication middleware to actually skip authentication.\n// This means even \"public\" servers that should not require authentication still have\n// authentication enforced on them.\nfunc TestRegression_ServerAuthenticationSkipNotConfigured(t *testing.T) {\n\t// The SkipsAuthenticationServer interface exists and is implemented by public.Server\n\t// but in internal/cmd/authn.go, when authenticationGRPC() is called, the\n\t// WithServerSkipsAuthentication option is never used to register servers.\n\n\t// This means:\n\t// 1. Public authentication methods (like ListAuthenticationMethods) should not require auth\n\t// 2. But there's no mechanism to bypass the AuthenticationRequiredInterceptor\n\t// 3. The skipped() function in middleware.go checks if a server implements\n\t//    SkipsAuthenticationServer, but servers are never registered with this option\n\n\t// Verify that WithServerSkipsAuthentication option exists\n\tvar opts []interface{}\n\t// This function exists but is never called in the registration code\n\t// opts = append(opts, grpc_middleware.WithServerSkipsAuthentication(publicServer))\n\n\t// Without calling WithServerSkipsAuthentication during setup, the middleware has no way\n\t// to know which servers should skip authentication, and the skipped() function will\n\t// always return false for the skipped servers slice check.\n\n\t// The expected behavior would be:\n\t// 1. Public servers implement SkipsAuthenticationServer\n\t// 2. They should be registered with WithServerSkipsAuthentication during middleware setup\n\t// 3. The middleware's skipped() function should check the interface AND the registered list\n\n\t// But currently step 2 is missing, so all servers require authentication\n\n\tt.Log(\"REGRESSION: Server-level authentication skip mechanism exists but is not configured\")\n\tt.Log(\"Public servers implement SkipsAuthenticationServer interface\")\n\tt.Log(\"But WithServerSkipsAuthentication is never called during middleware setup\")\n\tt.Log(\"This means public servers are incorrectly forced to require authentication\")\n}\n\n// TestRegression_CookieForwardingToGRPCMetadata tests the integration between\n// HTTP cookies and gRPC metadata forwarding for the gRPC-gateway.\nfunc TestRegression_CookieForwardingToGRPCMetadata(t *testing.T) {\n\t// The gRPC middleware expects cookies to be available as gRPC metadata\n\t// with the key \"grpcgateway-cookie\" to parse them properly\n\n\tconst clientToken = \"valid_token_xyz789\"\n\n\treq := httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://localhost/api/v1/flags\", nil)\n\treq.AddCookie(&http.Cookie{\n\t\tName:  \"flipt_client_token\",\n\t\tValue: clientToken,\n\t})\n\n\t// Convert HTTP cookies to gRPC metadata\n\tmd := method.ForwardCookies(context.Background(), req)\n\n\t// Check the actual structure of the returned metadata\n\tt.Logf(\"Forwarded metadata keys: %v\", md)\n\tt.Logf(\"Metadata content: %#v\", map[string][]string(md))\n\n\t// The gRPC middleware's cookieFromMetadata function expects:\n\t// md.Get(\"grpcgateway-cookie\") to return cookie header values\n\t// which it then parses with http.Cookie\n\n\tcookieHeaders := md.Get(\"grpcgateway-cookie\")\n\n\t// The issue: ForwardCookies should create a proper \"Cookie\" header string\n\t// that can be parsed by the gRPC middleware, but it doesn't do this correctly\n\n\tif len(cookieHeaders) == 0 {\n\t\tt.Error(\"REGRESSION: No grpcgateway-cookie metadata entry - Browser makes HTTP request with flipt_client_token cookie\n\t// 2. gRPC-gateway converts this to gRPC call\n\t// 3. cookieStr == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// The cookie header should contain the token\n\t\t\tif cookieStr == clientToken {\n\t\t\t\thasTokenCookie = COOKIE-BASED TOKEN EXTRACTION BUG\n   Location: internal/server/authn/method/http.go, ForwardCookies() function\n   Problem: The function iterates through cookie keys but always writes to the same metadata key,\n            causing token cookies to be lost or overwrite other cookies.\n\n   Bug Details (Line 49 of http.go):\n   ```\n   for _, key := range []string{stateCookieKey, tokenCookieKey} {\n       if cookie, err := req.Cookie(key); err == nil {\n           md[stateCookieKey] = []string{cookie.Value}  // BUG: Always uses stateCookieKey!\n       }\n   }\n   ```\n\n   Impact: Browser-based sessions fail because:\n   - Cookies with authentication tokens are not properly forwarded to gRPC middleware\n   - The gRPC middleware expects tokens via \"grpcgateway-cookie\" metadata\n   - Without proper forwarding, token extraction fails\n   - Requests that carry valid tokens in cookies are rejected as unauthenticated\n\n2. Browser makes HTTP request with flipt_client_token cookie\n\t// 2. gRPC-gateway converts this to gRPC call\n\t// 3.
